Importante sa mga Pilipina na maputi ang kanilang kilikili.	It’s important for Filipinas that their armpits are white.
In American English, it’s “panties” and “briefs” — in the Filipino	language, it’s panti and brip.
In Filipino conversations, it’s very common to hear Sinong may bertdey?	(Whose birthday is it?).

Notice the difference in pronunciation between bása (a verb meaning ‘to	read’) and basâ (an adjective meaning ‘wet’).
Notice the difference in the accents on the second syllable of each	differently defined word. The first meaning is more common.
